padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1218968">Arctic Archer</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-11">10/11/24 09:48</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Eau dâOmbre Leather (EDOL) is a very good, softer, and more mellow version of the original Ombre Leather (OG). <br />
<br />
While assessing this scent, Itâs important to contextualize EDOL in comparison to its predecessor. After all,  the OG is a modern masterpiece, an avant-garde take on leather fragrance. While most leather-scents, like Tom Ford's Tuscan Leather or in extreme, Guerlain Cuir Intense, fall under category of âfigurativesâ in Jean Claude-Ellenaâs modern classification of perfumes ( âfigurativesâ faithfully replicate the original scent, be it leather, roses or whatever),  OG takes a different approach.<br />
<br />
The OG Ombre Leather stands out as a pared-down, modern, and abstract interpretation of leatherâmuch sleeker and refined than something like Tuscan Leather, which has a more conventional leather feel. Enter EDOL, a reinterpretation that stays true to the OG but delivers a softer experience.<br />
<br />
EDOL opens with fresh notes of ginger and coriander, though they disappear quickly, leaving the heart notes. After about 30 minutes, what remains is a combination of the OG Ombre Leather mixed with vanilla. This addition makes the scent more approachable, lending it a smoothness that the OG doesnât have. Furthermore, within the first few hours, I detect a faint echo reminiscent of Tom Fordâs Fucking Fabulous, especially in the early stages. This is likely due to the vanilla-leather-powdery combination, which mirrors FFâs luxurious, slightly creamy texture.<br />
<br />
As the scent develops over a few hours, it settles into a warm, enveloping base of vanilla and amber (ambrofix), with a subtle echo of the OG. <br />
<br />
For an Eau de Toilette, the longevity is surprisingly good, lasting about eight hours on my skin. This is impressive for this kind of EdT. Good for day at work, without need of reapplication. <br />
<br />
In conclusion: EDOL offers a non-offensive, softer take on the OG Ombre Leather. Itâs ideal for everyday wear, whether at work or in casual settings. While it may lack the boldness of the OG, it delivers a refined, more approachable interpretation of the Ombre Leather DNAâperfect for those who loved the original but are looking for something smoother and more versatile. However, if you prefer a more avant-garde and abstract approach to leather, the OG remains the better choice.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95389"comment_id="2312245"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Tom-Ford/Eau-d-Ombre-Leather-95389.html?ccid=2312245#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2310869" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />

It's as masculine as it is feminine, but I can see more men wearing this than women.<br />

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2267160">Skzeratul</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-26">09/26/24 04:32</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Tried this at the mall at the Tom Ford section and I must say I really like this. It's a very easy to wear leather, entry level in my opinion, that turns to a slightly spicy vanilla scent. The leather definitely takes a step back in the dry down and you're mostly left with that vanilla. Longevity for me is great, around 8 or 9 hours. For me, sillage isn't the best, but I did smell it from time to time as I sat on my computer typing, and playing games. This was 3 to 4 hours after. Honestly I even hesitate to call this a flanker to Ombre Leather because I think they're very different. Eau d'Ombre Leather could be it's own fragrance. This is definitely better suited for nights and fall/winter, but I think this can also be pulled off during the cool days and in the spring. I look forward to owning this very soon.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95389"comment_id="2295523"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Tom-Ford/Eau-d-Ombre-Leather-95389.html?ccid=2295523#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2295355" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2289383" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Kallero"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1861210"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1861210.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Kallero" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2289383ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2289383" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.75); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1861210">Kallero</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-20">09/20/24 11:14</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I really don't care about other opinions here. This is one of my top fragrances in the rotation. It doesn't smell like Babycat, to me bbcat is trash, the incense note is a church bomb, a no-no for me. It reminds me of Spicebomb Extreme a bit because of that lingering vanilla but the notes that made me dislike Spicebomb are either not here or blended much better. This right here is sexy, sophisticated and lasts a long time. It has a deliciousness to it that's inviting and pleasant. It's like a waffle, you crave a bite but in this case you crave a sniff. It's also somehow fresh and deep. It has an amazing structure, from top to drydown it remains a super pleasant fragrance to take whiffs from. Like somebody said, you easily smell it on you even after a while and don't go noseblind to it like many other fragrances. Projection is superb as well. Probably not for everybody but god knows I'll be wearing this all year long. Most likely a safe blind buy.<br />
<br />
Scent - 9/10<br />
Projection - 8/10<br />
Price - 7/10<br />

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1211792">Atomikbomb_</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-05">09/05/24 19:12</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>My husband foisted his sample of this at me, because it's too vanillic for him. But...I'm kind of selfishly grateful, because I love this. <br />
<br />
I didn't care for Ombre Leather at all. It was extremely strong, and nearly a sour leather. I truly didn't enjoy it on anyone (my friend hosted a Christmas party and everyone tested it that night), nor on myself. (And now I have an unfortunate association with strong leather and Christmas punch). It was always overkill even with one spray, and even in the biting winter air. I just dislike it.<br />
<br />
However...wow...this is lovely. It's the same underlying leather note, but waaaaay less intense. The sour edges are smoothed out by the powdery vanilla, and it's extremely well tamed. In fact, today was hot, but one modest spray on wrists was still polite, and not suffocating in the heat. The weather just served to project the scent, but it's enjoyable. <br />
<br />
Cardamom is one of my very favorite notes, and it's used quite well here. I find that it can soar in heat without smothering people, and it rarely feels oppressive in fragrances (or food). Pairing with leather and vanilla is perfection. Still, probably more of a winter scent, but oddly ok and wearable at any time. <br />
<br />
This is easily unisex, I like it on my husband, but it's not really "him". Dare I say it...this really suits me. <br />
<br />
I won't buy this, because I just won't, and the price is prohibitive. What I might consider, is trying to score another free sample or two, or purchasing a couple to wear occasionally. One spray or two is sufficient, because performance is excellent. That way, I could have a little more without dropping crazy money on it.<br />
<br />
Overall? It's a little badass, but more of a softer, comforting leather, and less of an intimidating, villainous leather. Really, really damn good.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95389"comment_id="2273065"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Tom-Ford/Eau-d-Ombre-Leather-95389.html?ccid=2273065#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2272943" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2046807">SpanaUomo</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-05">09/05/24 11:48</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Tom Ford Noir Extreme Eau de Toilette  ?<br />
<br />
Well, I will start by saying that I am a big fan of Tom Ford perfumery.That said there are, of course, some I donât like, and there are some that I adore.<br />
Being two of them, actually my absolute favorites are Ombre Leather EdP, and Noir Extreme EdP.<br />
I also own and really enjoy Ombre Leather Parfum.<br />
I was very excited that there was a new Ombre Leather flanker, and when I learned that it was done by Sonia Constant I got even more excited.<br />
Today I got my nose on it. It was a quiet departure from the previous Ombre Leathers. I never smelled Babycat, to which it is being compared, and to me this would be a more suitable flanker to Noir Extreme. If you tone down the spiceness from Noir Extreme, take out the kulfi note this is what you get. And on my skin it projects more than the Noir Extreme edp. The Vanilla is done in a very right way, dry and pleasant, I usually donât like Vanilla note, but Tom Ford knows how to pull it off.<br />
But donât expect it be anything like previous Ombre Leathers.<br />
So if youâre a fan of Noir Extreme edp, and wished it was less spicy and more projecting you will definitely like this. <br />
And I can imagine it will layer extremely well with Ombre Leather and Noir flankers!<br />
As for me, who collects frags, I will definitely get it, but its not a "get it right away" fragrance for me.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95389"comment_id="2272681"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Tom-Ford/Eau-d-Ombre-Leather-95389.html?ccid=2272681#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2272461" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; The leather is a little more subtle on the top and stays till around the one hour mark. It slowly fades away into a sexy suede vibe backed with vanilla. As I get into the 2-3 hour mark, the leather is gone for the most part but am left with the beautiful vanilla/tobacco feeling......very much like Fortitude from Robert Graham. It's absolutely stunning. This sits around for the next 7+ hours.<br />
<br />
TF could have called this something other than Eau d'Ombre Leather. The leather is on top but isn't around as long as what you'd think....especially with "Leather" in the name. <br />
<br />
Overall I'm very impressed and shocked TF put something like this out. Some of releases TF has put out these last couple of years were dud's IMO. <br />
<br />
I'm glad I have this for the fall/winter because it's perfect for the colder weather!<br />

if you are not sure on buying the 2018 ombre leather because of the animalic smell, the leather, the more harsher opening with a statement etc iâd suggest you trying this one. <br />

Not a blind buy, never blind buy!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95389"comment_id="2260438"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Tom-Ford/Eau-d-Ombre-Leather-95389.html?ccid=2260438#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2260049" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2191906">chrisivE</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-24">08/24/24 20:54</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Eau d'Ombre Leather by Tom Ford Review<br />
<br />
As someone who considers Ombre Leather Parfum my signature scent, I was particularly excited to try Eau d'Ombre Leather. The opening immediately reminded me of Oud Wood, likely due to the presence of Ambrofixâ¢. This synthetic compound mimics the warmth of amber but with a stronger, more pronounced edge. The similarity to Oud Wood is further enhanced by the shared notes of vanilla and cardamom, though here, the combination with ginger creates an unexpected twistâa sweet aroma that evokes the comforting scent of banana bread or ginger cookies.<br />
<br />
In Eau d'Ombre Leather, the leather note is much more subdued compared to the intense, in-your-face leather of the original. Itâs subtle and plays a background role, making this fragrance feel distinctly different. While Ombre Leather Parfum exudes a "mysterious, slightly scary sexy" vibe, Eau d'Ombre Leather feels more "friendly and inviting sexy." Itâs approachable and warm, without losing that touch of sophistication.<br />
<br />
I didnât distinctly pick up on the coriander, but it likely blends seamlessly with the other spices, enhancing their overall spicy profile without standing out on its own. The result is a fragrance thatâs both complex and well-balanced, with a smooth transition between its notes.<br />
<br />
One of the standout features of Eau d'Ombre Leather is its longevity. It lasts impressively long on the skin, keeping its inviting, subtly spicy character throughout the day. For those who appreciate the original Ombre Leather but want something a bit more approachable and versatile, Eau d'Ombre Leather is an excellent choice.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1417787">mlke</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-23">08/23/24 10:37</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>There's no ambery, sour jasmine note from the original here. I feel like that floral, slightly indolic and radiantly warm heart made it elegant and refined. That's all gone from this version and replaced with a fresh, somewhat hollow and aromatic vanilla. The cardamom will stick out for most people. I like the freshness contrasted against the smoky, rubbery notes in the first few minutes- but that cool, ozonic edge only gives it an interesting life for the first half hour. The leather here is smoother, more matte and finely textured (suede-like), and the smokiness is allowed to punch through the aromatics more noticeably. After a little while it feels very simple and even though the theme of dark leather is still somewhat "niche", it feels lacking in character a bit. Somewhat flat and one-dimensional for a vanilla. The leather note itself is nice, and I like that I can't corner it into a standard leather material like birch tar or safraleine, but I feel like they should have done more with it. It gets woodier as time goes on, which I'm indifferent to. It's probably more accessible, but not as enchanting as the original. edit: a part of this really does smell like a less dynamic version of animalique by byredo without the smoky rubber parts</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Ombre leather, and Ombre leather parfum, have the same DNA. The indolic jasmine, the gamma/beta ionones, isobutyl quinoline etc. but they are different.<br />
This!! This is basically a blast of ginger then the dry down to lost cherry.<br />
The guaiac wood smokiness, with some spice and vanilla. That's it!! There's no sexy florals or deep suede/leather.<br />
And I know this is supposed to be "eau de..." But they could have kept the sexy narcotic DNA of the previous two, and made it more light and aquatic.<br />
<br />
So disappointing. Vanilla, ginger, clove and guaiac wood. And some musk. No leather.<br />

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1477503">Siprian85</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-03">08/03/24 17:09</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Fragrance Notes:<br />
<br />
Top Notes:<br />
Ginger, Cardamom, Coriander.<br />
<br />
Mid Notes:<br />
Leather, Vanilla.<br />
<br />
Base Notes:<br />
Ambrofix.<br />
<br />
 Fragrance Review<br />
<br />
First thoughts, this is a milder version of Ombre Leather. Contains a warm spice scent, burnt rubber/gasoline in the opening and has a tobacco in the drydown. <br />
<br />
- Eau D'ombre Leather starts similar to Ombre Leather, the difference is that the opening smells more like rubber/ Gasoline.<br />
<br />
- I sprayed a total of 5 times. Twice behind each ear, twice on the front of neck, and once in front of my chest. The longevity is good, it lasts approximately 8-10 hours on my skin, projects for about an arms length for 1-2 hours before turning into a skin scent. It does however lasts a few days on my clothes. <br />
(Depends on skin types)<br />
<br />
Overall Rating  (8/10)<br />
A suitable leather fragrance for begineers who are slowly getting used to leather notes, as well as Tobacco. The opening and mid notes has an intense Violet Leaf + Cardamom + Leather combination which may be off putting for some people. I would suggest trying this on your skin first before buying it blindly.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95389"comment_id="2238049"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Tom-Ford/Eau-d-Ombre-Leather-95389.html?ccid=2238049#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2235658" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Bought my first bottle of the OG OmbrÃ© Leather (Signature line) back on release.. bought another 3 bottles of this gem since then.<br />
Parfum version had a lighter "twist" instead of heavier.. I quite liked that..<br />

Ambrofix (Ambroxan but manufactured by Givaudan that has a "Pine-ish" note instead of "Tobacco-ish" that [Ambroxan] has)<br />
plus the ginger and vanilla.<br />

As Fragrantica suggests about Oud wood (quoting): <br />
Royal, transcendent, and monumental interpretation of  Ì¶oÌ¶uÌ¶dÌ¶    leather*<br />

if you ask me.. I'm all about this.. and I hope I'm right. <br />

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1211792">Atomikbomb_</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-05">09/05/24 19:12</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>My husband foisted his sample of this at me, because it's too vanillic for him. But...I'm kind of selfishly grateful, because I love this. <br />
<br />
I didn't care for Ombre Leather at all. It was extremely strong, and nearly a sour leather. I truly didn't enjoy it on anyone (my friend hosted a Christmas party and everyone tested it that night), nor on myself. (And now I have an unfortunate association with strong leather and Christmas punch). It was always overkill even with one spray, and even in the biting winter air. I just dislike it.<br />
<br />
However...wow...this is lovely. It's the same underlying leather note, but waaaaay less intense. The sour edges are smoothed out by the powdery vanilla, and it's extremely well tamed. In fact, today was hot, but one modest spray on wrists was still polite, and not suffocating in the heat. The weather just served to project the scent, but it's enjoyable. <br />
<br />
Cardamom is one of my very favorite notes, and it's used quite well here. I find that it can soar in heat without smothering people, and it rarely feels oppressive in fragrances (or food). Pairing with leather and vanilla is perfection. Still, probably more of a winter scent, but oddly ok and wearable at any time. <br />
<br />
This is easily unisex, I like it on my husband, but it's not really "him". Dare I say it...this really suits me. <br />
<br />
I won't buy this, because I just won't, and the price is prohibitive. What I might consider, is trying to score another free sample or two, or purchasing a couple to wear occasionally. One spray or two is sufficient, because performance is excellent. That way, I could have a little more without dropping crazy money on it.<br />
<br />
Overall? It's a little badass, but more of a softer, comforting leather, and less of an intimidating, villainous leather. Really, really damn good.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95389"comment_id="2273065"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Tom-Ford/Eau-d-Ombre-Leather-95389.html?ccid=2273065#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2298465" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;
